    (function () {

        const ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES = [
            {
                url: "https://cdn.cookielaw.org/consent/tcf.stub.js",

                    charSet: "UTF-8",

            }
        };
        const BANNER_SDK = {
            url: "https://cdn.cookielaw.org/scripttemplates/202404.1.0/otBannerSdk.js",
            options: {},
        }

        const countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {"countries":["ES","MX","PH","TH","TR"]};

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter of the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_84" title="Chapter 84">Chapter 84</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Zombies</b> are corpses capable of self-movement and other sentient actions. Well-known in superstitions and literature throughout the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a>, they can be created in actuality through at least one method: infusing corpses with shadows via the <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kage no Mi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Creation_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Creation-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>, the current wielder of the Kage Kage no Mi, is known to have created over one thousand zombies as subordinates. The vast majority of these inhabited his island-ship of <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, and comprised a mix of <a href="/wiki/Humans" title="Humans">humans</a>, wildlife, and <a href="/wiki/Race" title="Race">strange creatures</a> that resembled beasts and monsters commonly found in mythology and horror stories. To create more powerful zombies, Moria enlisted the services of Dr. <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a>, who used his medical expertise to enhance them into stiched up creations he called <b>marios</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>没人形</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>マリオ</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Mario</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Death Doll"; VIZ and Funimation dub: "Marionettes")</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Hogback_reveal_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hogback_reveal-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The zombies of Thriller Bark were commanded by the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates#Organization" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Mysterious Four</a>, which consisted of Moria, Dr. Hogback, <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a>. While Hogback, Absalom, and Perona had a varying degree of command over the creatures, Moria alone had absolute control over all of the zombies.
</p><p>The zombies remained active for a span of at least ten years after the establishment of Thriller Bark. However, while battling the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, Moria implanted the shadows of his zombie army within himself as a last ditch effort to defeat the Straw Hats and their allies. Without any shadows animating them, the corpses all became lifeless once again.<sup id="cite_ref-Shadow_Asgard_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shadow_Asgard-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Overview">Overview</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Zombie_Shadow_Explanation.png/revision/latest?cb=20240727040615" class="image"><img alt="Zombie Shadow Explanation" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Zombie_Shadow_Explanation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240727040615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="179" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zombie Shadow Explanation.png" data-image-key="Zombie_Shadow_Explanation.png" data-relevant="1" /></a> 	 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zombie_Shadow_Explanation.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A strong shadow combined with a strong corpse can create an even stronger zombie.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Basic zombies are created by the power of Moria's Kage Kage no Mi. First, Moria captures a victim. Using his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> powers, Moria grabs a hold of the victim's shadow and cuts it from the owner using a pair of scissors. Moria then forms a contract of obedience with the shadow and implants it into a corpse.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Creation_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Creation-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A zombie created through this process retains the personality and fighting techniques of the person whom the shadow originally belonged to. The zombie's physical strength, however, depends on the body used. When a strong shadow and a strong corpse are combined, an even stronger zombie is created. For this reason, during Moria's rule over Thriller Bark, Hogback collected and stitched together hundreds of corpses to make strong creatures. This was best seen via the Zombie Generals, whose bodies were created from the various remains of famous warriors.
</p><p>Zombies made with shadows of people of high levels of strength can be difficult to control at first, but they eventually fall in line. While initially retaining the personality of the shadow's owner, the zombie will eventually even disregard that person's heartfelt beliefs and solemn oaths as they fall into total obedience. For example, <a href="/wiki/Inuppe" title="Inuppe">Inuppe</a>, the zombie with <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s shadow, initially upheld Sanji's oath to never harm a lady and even attacked his fellow zombies when they tried to attack <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>. Later that same night, he attacked <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> without giving her gender a second thought.
</p><p>The victim whose shadow was stolen falls into a two-day coma. The only known way to awaken them early is to coax them awake with their personal vices. Even though separated, the person and the shadow are still a single being, meaning that if the person dies, their shadow will die as well, along with the zombie the shadow was placed inside of. Because of this, Moria prefers that his victims remain alive. During his rule over Thriller Bark, he had his victims placed back onto their ships and set adrift to ensure that they survived while remaining unable to come back and retake their shadows.
</p><p>Though there were a lot of zombies on Thriller Bark, they would sometimes need to be replaced. This would happen when the original owners of the shadows animating them died, when Moria removed their shadows himself, or when the zombies were "purified" by ingesting salt, which caused their shadow to fly out and return to its original owner. To replace these losses, newer zombies were created from the entire corpses or individual body parts of the older zombies that were lost.<sup id="cite_ref-new_number_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-new_number-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Zombie_Gallery">Zombie Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Many of the creatures on Thriller Bark had a number written on them. The importance of this number was to tell which rank or groups they belonged to. The numbers were usually written on the creature itself - either on the head, stomach, back or side of the creature. A few of the zombies had it written on a band around their arm.
</p><p>While the numbers represented which rank a zombie would be placed in, newer zombies could be assigned a lower number despite the order they were created in relation to other zombies. This was because these newer zombies were created to fill in the holes left by zombies that were either purified or destroyed.<sup id="cite_ref-new_number_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-new_number-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The numbers ranges of the Zombie ranks were as follows:
</p>
<ul><li>Numbers 0 - 199 = Wild Zombies.</li>
<li>Numbers 200 - 399 = Surprise Zombies.</li>
<li>Numbers 400 - 799 = Zombie Soldiers.</li>
<li>Numbers 800 - 899 = General Zombies.</li>
<li>Number 900 = Special-Ranked Zombie</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Overall_Strength">Overall Strength</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>While a zombie inherits the skills and memories of the shadow animating them, they do not inherit any Devil Fruit powers if the shadow belonged to a Devil Fruit user. Moria, can make up for their inability to perform any Devil Fruit based attacks to an extent by implanting his own shadow into the zombie's shadow. From there, he can manipulate the zombie's shape via a reverse form of shadow puppetry called <b>Kage Kakumei</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_puppet_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_puppet-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Zombies are completely impervious to conventional methods such as beheading. Though some of them sometimes act like they are in pain when hit or feel tired as if they lost stamina, all zombies are actually immune to such things. When a zombie expresses such things it is not because they are in pain or tired, it is because the shadow animating them still remembers such feelings when they were originally attached to their original owners. Eventually, these memories of feeling pain and such will be completely forgotten thus rendering any zombie capable of functioning without expressing such things at all. Zombies are thus tireless creations who seemingly cannot be stopped no matter how hard or how long one fights against them.
</p><p>While zombies seem to be unbeatable creatures, they do have weaknesses. When salt is thrown into a zombie's mouth, the shadow moving the corpse is detached and the zombie is purified. Because salt is a property of sea water and since the shadow was attached due to a Devil Fruit power, the shadow is naturally released. Though depending on the size of the zombie (eg. Oars) a bag of salt isn't enough to purify the zombie. A zombie's body may also be burned in order to release the shadow, as seen when Zoro set the samurai Ryuma alight, returning Brook's shadow to him once the body had finished burning. Zombies also remain "alive" as long the person whose shadow they use remains alive. If the person dies, so will his shadow. According to Brook, this is because the shadow and the person, though separated, are still of one soul. For this, Moria and his associates ensure that their victims will not die.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Salt_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Salt-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Another weakness could be attributed as an error by the zombie's creator. The zombies strength are based on putting strong shadows into stronger Mario's to create the strongest zombies. However should the creators misjudge the strength of the original shadow's owner, they may actually place the shadow in a weaker corpse, thus creating a zombie which is inferior to the original. An example would be <a href="/wiki/Inuppe" title="Inuppe">Inuppe</a>, who possessed <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s shadow. Though Sanji is a fighter with strength comparable to <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a>, due to the confusion caused by his <a href="/wiki/Wanted_Poster" class="mw-redirect" title="Wanted Poster">Wanted Poster</a>, they mistook him for a grunt and put his shadow in an ill-suited Wild Zombie. Even though Inuppe possessed all the other strengths of a zombie, due to having a stubby body unsuited to wield Sanji's <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style" title="Black Leg Style">Black Leg Style</a>, it actually fell short of Sanji's full potential.
</p><p>While a zombie's greatest strength is being not able to feel pain, it is also their greatest weak point. Because a zombie is unable to feel pain, they are unable gauge how badly damaged their body can or has become in a battle. This action inadvertently leads to their downfall as they would continue fighting non-stop without taking any time to heal or fix their wounds. With this, their wounds can build up and become massive, and can eventually cause a zombie to become unable to move their body at all. They can still function even when their bodies are completely broken. However, they can no longer fight despite still having the will to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_wound_weakness_1_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_wound_weakness_1-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_wound_weakness_2_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_wound_weakness_2-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_wound_weakness_3_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_wound_weakness_3-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Types_of_Zombies">Types of Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wild_Zombies">Wild Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Wild_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914023829" class="image"><img alt="Wild Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="96" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wild Zombies.png" data-image-key="Wild_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Wild_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914023829" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Wild_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914023829" class="image"><img alt="Wild Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Wild_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914023829" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="96" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wild Zombies.png" data-image-key="Wild_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Wild_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914023829" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wild_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Wild Zombies in Thriller Bark's Woods.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><b>Wild Zombies</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>動物</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ワイルド</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>ゾンビ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Wairudo Zonbi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Animal Zombies")</span> are zombies that consist of mainly stitched-up animals that are far less dead-like compared to the other zombies of Thriller Bark. They are capable of talking and are mostly commanded by <a href="/wiki/Perona" title="Perona">Perona</a>. Most of them are zombies created by Hogback based on Perona's stuffed toys per her request. A number of these were first seen by <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a> lurking in the woods.<sup id="cite_ref-TB_woods_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TB_woods-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, a large number of them waylaid Usopp, Nami, and Chopper in Perona's garden after they escaped from their transport coffin.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Wonderland_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Wonderland-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> The animals, upon seeing them free, attempted to capture them. They were however stopped by the new penguin zombie. After being beaten several times by the dog penguin, they were commanded by Absalom, who had arrived there, to not harm Nami. They replied to him saying that they only obey Perona per Moria's order. They however decide to back down as Absalom reminds them to fear him also as he takes out the dog penguin.<sup id="cite_ref-Absalom_order_animal_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Absalom_order_animal-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Despite being animals, they fight with normal weapons such as swords, axes, and maces.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soldier_Zombies">Soldier Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024001" class="image"><img alt="Soldier Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Soldier Zombies.png" data-image-key="Soldier_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914024001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024001" class="image"><img alt="Soldier Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914024001" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Soldier Zombies.png" data-image-key="Soldier_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/ce/Soldier_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130914024001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Soldier_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Soldier Zombies rising from their graves.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The zombies serving as the basic grunt soldiers of Moria's army are the <b>Soldier Zombies</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>兵士</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ソルジャー</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>ゾンビ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Sorujā Zonbi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. They are generally commanded by <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a> but can be ordered around by other members of the Mysterious Four as well, such as Perona. They have great respect for their leader, Absalom, however, they are not afraid to tell him that he is a pervert, much to his dismay. They are found throughout Thriller Bark but a large number of them reside in the graveyard in front of the Mast Mansion.
</p><p>Though most of the Soldier Zombies are generally grunts with no distinguishing traits other than design, there are some that stand out more than others. Cindry appears to belong to this group of zombies, even though she seems somewhat different from them both in design and mannerisms. Moria's little errand zombies, Gyoro, Nin, and Bao, naturally fall under this category; however, they're more like helpers rather than grunt soldiers.
</p><p>A group of Soldier Zombies that reside in the graveyard attacked the carriage Nami, Usopp, and Chopper were in after Hildon and his companions left them.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_intro_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_intro-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> A great number of these have been seen with numbers either printed on their bodies or on arm bands. The numbers from 408, to 767 have been seen on these creatures.
</p><p>These zombies apparently have distinct personalities of sorts. They are apparently helpful to one another as seen when Chopper knocked one zombie's head off and another handed it back to him. The zombies are afraid of fire and in reply called Usopp a pyromaniac for attacking them with a fire star. Despite normally limping and moaning around like typical zombies, they are capable of running at great speeds. Unfortunately, they tire out easily.
</p><p>Later, the rest of the Straw Hats encountered these creatures, though their reactions to them were completely different from Nami, Usopp, and Chopper's previous encounters.<sup id="cite_ref-600B_Jackpot_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-600B_Jackpot-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> After being completely defeated by the Straw Hats, the zombies inadvertently revealed to them about their attack on the latter's friends. For this, the zombies were shoved head first back into their graves.
</p><p>Later, after the zombies pulled themselves out of the ground, they received orders from Absalom to prepare to attack the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-Absalom_corp_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Absalom_corp-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Absalom reassured the zombies they actually need not fear being burnt, fatigued, or pained, as it is all in their minds as they are dead. The zombies, with the advent of the attack about to begin, were joined by the majority of the other Soldier Zombies in the island and gathered in the area in front of the Mast Mansion. There they started dancing the disco complete with a disco ball.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Disco_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Disco-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the attack commenced, it was later revealed that a massive number of these zombies were purified by <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a>. Their lifeless corpses were littered across the island and were reported to Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Soldier_Defeat_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Soldier_Defeat-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> This number of purified creatures, along with other Surprise and Wild Zombies, was later further increased by the Straw Hats' assault to take back their shadows.<sup id="cite_ref-Hildon_reports_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hildon_reports-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The remaining Soldier Zombies stayed far away from the Mast Mansion and watched the gigantic battle between the Straw Hats and <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a>. Upon seeing Oars being beaten up by Luffy and hearing that their master, Moria, had entered the battle, they were shocked in disbelief of what was happening. After Oars was pulverized, they were ecstatic to see that their master survived. However, their joy, as well as their existence, was put to an end as they watched in horror as Moria took away the shadows animating them to power himself up.<sup id="cite_ref-Shadow_Asgard_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shadow_Asgard-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> The Soldier Zombies, as well as the other zombies, then returned to being lifeless corpses.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Surprise_Zombies">Surprise Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20180719035207" class="image"><img alt="Bear Skin and Painting Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bear Skin and Painting Zombies.png" data-image-key="Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180719035207" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20180719035207" class="image"><img alt="Bear Skin and Painting Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180719035207" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bear Skin and Painting Zombies.png" data-image-key="Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180719035207" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bear_Skin_and_Painting_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Bear's Skin Rug and Painting Zombies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><b>Surprise Zombies</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">びっくりゾンビ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Bikkuri Zonbi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> are disguised as various objects scattered around Thriller Bark. The majority of them seem to be stitched up pieces of skin and cloth sewn together and attached to picture frames. These zombies hide within their picture frames in order to disguise themselves as portraits and when they attack enemies, they come out of their picture frames fully with only a part of them still attached to the picture frames. These zombies appear to be based on the commonly used concept in horror stories of portraits that look as if their eyes are capable of looking around and moving.
</p><p>Other Surprise Zombies include various zombies disguised as things other than paintings. These include pieces of taxidermy, such as the mounted head of a pig to even an entire wall with a human's face stretched across it.
</p><p>Several of these Surprise Zombies were seen in the dining hall and hallways of Dr. Hogback's mansion disguised as paintings.<sup id="cite_ref-Surprise_Zombie_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Surprise_Zombie-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> The numbers 204, 217, and 280 were seen printed on three of these zombies. The painting zombies in the dining hall as well the bear skin rug were later defeated by Luffy and the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-Paint_Zombies_vs._5_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paint_Zombies_vs._5-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="General_Zombies">General Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/General_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20221116201059" class="image"><img alt="General Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="60" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="General Zombies.png" data-image-key="General_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/General_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221116201059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/General_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20221116201059" class="image"><img alt="General Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/General_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221116201059" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="60" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="General Zombies.png" data-image-key="General_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/General_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221116201059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:General_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The General Zombies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <b>General Zombies</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>将軍</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ジェネラル</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>ゾンビ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Jeneraru Zonbi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> are a specialized group of zombies commanded by Absalom. They first appeared rising up from their resting places when Absalom beckoned them to commence the attack on the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_general_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_general-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> They are a completely different level of zombies compared to the generic ones. According to Buhichuck, they are built from the corpses of renowned and strong warriors such as legendary samurai and knight leaders.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Among their ranks, they include a drunk zombie named John, a four-armed zombie, a large centaur like zombie with elephant feet, a samurai zombie with a toothbrush mustache called Jigoro, and several other zombies wearing suits of armor. They have been seen with numbers ranging throughout the 800's place.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_Ranked_Zombies">Special Ranked Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A <b>Special Zombie</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>特別</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>スペシャル</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>ゾンビ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Supesharu Zonbi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> is a type of zombie that is vastly stronger than a regular one. However, only one of these was made, Oars. The original plan by Moria was to create more of these in the future by stealing shadows from more powerful people, and placing them in more powerful corpses.<sup id="cite_ref-SZ_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SZ-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Zombies">Marineford Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Marine_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20240727040855" class="image"><img alt="Marine Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="240" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marine Zombies.png" data-image-key="Marine_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Marine_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240727040855" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Marine_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20240727040855" class="image"><img alt="Marine Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Marine_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240727040855" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="240" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marine Zombies.png" data-image-key="Marine_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/62/Marine_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240727040855" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marine_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marine Zombies defeated by Jinbe with sea water.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Marineford zombies are very different from their Thriller Bark counterparts in that they were Marines or pirates that died during the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_War" class="mw-redirect" title="Whitebeard War">war</a> and were revived by Moria's Kage Kage no Mi powers seemingly on the spot, without any known help from Hogback. These zombies had stitches and bandages on them, which made it unclear who exactly put them back together for Moria. It also remains unknown where Moria obtained the shadows necessary to create a large army of zombies.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Zombies">Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>See also&#32;the associated category: <a href="/wiki/Category:Zombies" title="Category:Zombies">Zombies</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wild_Zombies_2">Wild Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kumashi">Kumashi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230118162847" class="image"><img alt="Kumashi Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="289" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kumashi Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230118162847" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230118162847" class="image"><img alt="Kumashi Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230118162847" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="289" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kumashi Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230118162847" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kumashi_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kumashi</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Kumashi is a strange looking stuffed bear that was first seen in Perona's room when her ghosts came back to her body.<sup id="cite_ref-Stuffed_Bear_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stuffed_Bear-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Perona tells it that it should talk less if it wants to continue working for her since she finds its voice uncute. As a result, he wears a surgical mask around his mouth. He is based off of the stuffed toy bear that Perona brought with her when she met Hogback ten years prior to the current storyline.<sup id="cite_ref-Toy_Kumashi_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toy_Kumashi-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> He served as the commander of the Wild Zombies under Perona's command.
</p><p>He first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_449" title="Chapter 449">Chapter 449</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_343" title="Episode 343">Episode 343</a>. He is voiced by Hiroshi Iwasaki in Japanese and Ray Hurd in the FUNimation English dub.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hippo_Gentleman">Hippo Gentleman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116130714" class="image"><img alt="Hippo Gentleman Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hippo Gentleman Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220116130714" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116130714" class="image"><img alt="Hippo Gentleman Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220116130714" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hippo Gentleman Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220116130714" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hippo_Gentleman_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hippo Gentleman</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Hippo_Gentleman" title="Hippo Gentleman">Hippo Gentleman</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p><b>Hippo Gentleman</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">カバ紳士</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kaba Shinshi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> is a large zombie that is basically a hippo's head attached to a human's body. He was first seen in the group of Wild Zombies that appeared in Perona's wonder garden.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Wonderland_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Wonderland-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> During the attack in the garden, he was the one that specifically tried to attack Nami. Later, during Usopp's battle with Perona, he appeared suddenly to seek revenge against Usopp for purifying Kumashi.
</p><p>His appearance may be based on a toy hippo obtained by Perona sometime ago that was a product of <a href="/wiki/Wapol" title="Wapol">Wapol</a>'s toy factory made through his <a href="/wiki/Baku_Baku_no_Mi" title="Baku Baku no Mi">Baku Baku no Mi</a> powers.<sup id="cite_ref-Toy_hippo_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toy_hippo-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> He first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_451" title="Chapter 451">Chapter 451</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_345" title="Episode 345">Episode 345</a>. He is voiced by Eiji Takemoto in Japanese.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hildon">Hildon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Hildon_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119071910" class="image"><img alt="Hildon Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hildon Portrait.png" data-image-key="Hildon_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Hildon_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071910" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Hildon_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119071910" class="image"><img alt="Hildon Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Hildon_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071910" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hildon Portrait.png" data-image-key="Hildon_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Hildon_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071910" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hildon_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hildon</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Hildon" title="Hildon">Hildon</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Hildon is a vampire-like creature that met up with Nami, Usopp, and Chopper. He has the number 21 printed over his right eye. Unlike most Wild Zombies, that is those with numbers between 1 and 199, he does not serve under Perona, but instead is one of Absalom's minions. <sup id="cite_ref-Hildon_servant_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hildon_servant-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He also appears to serve as the messenger on Thriller Bark as he goes about informing the Mysterious Four of various occurrences on the island.
</p><p>He first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_444" title="Chapter 444">Chapter 444</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_339" title="Episode 339">Episode 339</a>. He is voiced by Taiki Matsuno in Japanese and Jerry Jewell in the FUNimation English dub.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Risky_Brothers">Risky Brothers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130703191226" class="image"><img alt="Risky Brothers (Zombies) Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Risky Brothers (Zombies) Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130703191226" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130703191226" class="image"><img alt="Risky Brothers (Zombies) Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130703191226" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Risky Brothers (Zombies) Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Risky_Brothers_%28Zombies%29_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130703191226" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Risky_Brothers_(Zombies)_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Risky Brothers</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Risky_Brothers_(Zombie)" class="mw-redirect" title="Risky Brothers (Zombie)">Risky Brothers (Zombie)</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>They are a duo of zombie squirrels that serve Perona. Their names, personalities, and shadows come from the <a href="/wiki/Risky_Brothers" title="Risky Brothers">Risky Brothers</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Rolling_Pirates" title="Rolling Pirates">Rolling Pirates</a>. They were responsible for bringing Nami, Usopp, and Chopper to Gecko Moria to have their shadows removed.
</p><p>They first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_451" title="Chapter 451">Chapter 451</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_344" title="Episode 344">Episode 344</a>. They are voiced by Yūsuke Numata and Tamotsu Nishiwaki in Japanese; and are voiced by Brandon Jerome Bristowe and Ian Moore in the FUNimation English dub.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Penguin_Zombie_Trio">Penguin Zombie Trio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6b/Penguin_Trio.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20180719023016" class="image"><img alt="Penguin Trio" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Penguin Trio.PNG" data-image-key="Penguin_Trio.PNG" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6b/Penguin_Trio.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180719023016" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6b/Penguin_Trio.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20180719023016" class="image"><img alt="Penguin Trio" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6b/Penguin_Trio.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180719023016" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Penguin Trio.PNG" data-image-key="Penguin_Trio.PNG" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6b/Penguin_Trio.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180719023016" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Penguin_Trio.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Penguin Trio</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Inuppe" title="Inuppe">Inuppe</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>The <b>Penguin Zombie Trio</b> (ペンギンゾンビトリオ <i>Pengin zonbi torio</i>) are a trio of penguin zombies that were first seen by Usopp, Nami, and Chopper.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Wonderland_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Wonderland-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> They originally consisted of a duo and called themselves the <b>Penguin Zombie Duo</b> (ペンギンゾンビコンビ <i>Pengin zonbi konbi</i>, literally "Penguin Zombie Combi(nation)"). One of the original members is a one-eyed penguin with blonde hair and a scar over his left eye. He wears a newsboy cap and a red bowtie. The other original member is a penguin with what appear to be human lips stitched onto where his beak should be. He wears a top hat and a scarf. The newcomer, Inuppe, is a penguin with a dog's face stitched to its body that wears a checkered hat. He has the same personality and attributes as <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> as he was created using Sanji's shadow. While their numbers have yet to be clearly seen, they do however introduce themselves as one, two, and three.
</p><p>They first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_451" title="Chapter 451">Chapter 451</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_345" title="Episode 345">Episode 345</a>. The bowtie penguin and scarf penguin are voiced by Yuta Kasuya and Takahiro Fujimoto in Japanese. Inuppe is voiced by Hiroaki Hirata in Japanese and Eric Vale in English.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Cerberus">Cerberus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ed/Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20180714234700" class="image"><img alt="Cerberus Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Cerberus Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ed/Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180714234700" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ed/Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20180714234700" class="image"><img alt="Cerberus Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ed/Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180714234700" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Cerberus Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ed/Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180714234700" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Cerberus_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Cerberus</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Cerberus" title="Cerberus">Cerberus</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p><b>Cerberus</b> (ケルベロス <i>Keruberosu</i>) is a three-headed dog of sorts that Nami, Usopp, and Chopper encountered after falling to the bottom of a moat filled with a bunch of skulls.<sup id="cite_ref-Cerb_intro_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cerb_intro-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He was the first Thriller Bark creature the Straw Hats encountered on Thriller Bark. It resembles the legendary <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cerberus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cerberus">Cerberus</a> of Greek mythology.
</p><p>It first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_444" title="Chapter 444">Chapter 444</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_339" title="Episode 339">Episode 339</a>. It is voiced by Keiji Hirai in the Japanese anime.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Unigaro">Unigaro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130604225938" class="image"><img alt="Unigaro Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="219" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Unigaro Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604225938" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130604225938" class="image"><img alt="Unigaro Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604225938" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="219" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Unigaro Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604225938" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unigaro_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Unigaro</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Unigaro" title="Unigaro">Unigaro</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p><b>Unigaro</b><sup id="cite_ref-BlueDeep_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BlueDeep-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> is a stitched up horse that looks like a dead unicorn. He has the number 42 printed on its right side. He was first seen frolicking with a number of other creatures in the forest.<sup id="cite_ref-TB_woods_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TB_woods-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He was later seen drinking with a tree named <a href="/wiki/MocDonald" title="MocDonald">MocDonald</a> with the number 115 by Luffy and the rest of the Straw Hats that were travelling with him.<sup id="cite_ref-Tree_and_Unicorn_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tree_and_Unicorn-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He was then caught by Franky and refused to join Luffy's crew.
</p><p>He first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_445" title="Chapter 445">Chapter 445</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_345" title="Episode 345">Episode 345</a>. He is voiced by Hiroshi Okamoto in Japanese.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Human-faced_Trees">Human-faced Trees</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
