<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130604224554" class="image"><img alt="MocDonald Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="317" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MocDonald Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604224554" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130604224554" class="image"><img alt="MocDonald Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604224554" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="317" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MocDonald Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604224554" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MocDonald_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">MocDonald</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/MocDonald" title="MocDonald">MocDonald</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>These various zombie trees have human faces and limbs apparently stitched directly to their trunks and roots. Three of these have so far been seen frolicking with a number of other creatures in the forest.<sup id="cite_ref-TB_woods_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TB_woods-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Two of these have numbers 115 and 36 printed on their trunks.
</p><p>The tree with the number 115 named <b>MocDonald</b><sup id="cite_ref-BlueDeep_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BlueDeep-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> was later seen drinking with a unicorn named Unigaro by Luffy and the rest of the Straw Hats who weren't at Dr. Hogback's mansion at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-Tree_and_Unicorn_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tree_and_Unicorn-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> After Luffy and Franky caught the "Geezer Tree" and the unicorn respectively, Luffy attempted to ask the tree to join their crew. This attempt however was stopped by Zoro and Sanji.
</p><p>The human-trees first appeared in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_445" title="Chapter 445">Chapter 445</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_345" title="Episode 345">Episode 345</a>. MocDonald is voiced by He first debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_445" title="Chapter 445">Chapter 445</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_345" title="Episode 345">Episode 345</a>. He is voiced by Eiji Takemoto in Japanese and Aaron Roberts in the English dub.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Spider_Mice">Spider Mice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Spider_Mice_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130625204057" class="image"><img alt="Spider Mice Zombies" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Spider Mice Zombies.png" data-image-key="Spider_Mice_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Spider_Mice_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130625204057" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Spider_Mice_Zombies.png/revision/latest?cb=20130625204057" class="image"><img alt="Spider Mice Zombies" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Spider_Mice_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130625204057" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Spider Mice Zombies.png" data-image-key="Spider_Mice_Zombies.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Spider_Mice_Zombies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130625204057" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Spider_Mice_Zombies.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Zombies 196 and 24; two Spider Mice.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <b>Spider Mice</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">スパイダーマウス</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Supaidā Mausu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> are a group of zombies under the direct supervision of Tararan.<sup id="cite_ref-Spider_Mice_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spider_Mice-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> They are stitched-together mice or rats with spider legs grafted to them. They specialize in sneak attacks, and are the ones who had been kidnapping the Straw Hats one by one. According to Tararan, there are over five hundred of them on the island. Like Tararan, they also can produce webbing. Their zombie numbers are prefixed by an "S" for "spider".
</p><p>A large number of them attacked Franky and Robin, only to be scared off by their master's defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-Mice_Run_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mice_Run-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Three spider mice appeared in Moria's dance hall to report Tararan's defeat to the Mysterious Four. Absalom then ordered them to take Luffy's body back to the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Mice_Report_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mice_Report-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Carriage_Drivers">Carriage Drivers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png/revision/latest?cb=20231129024717" class="image"><img alt="Zombie Carriage Drivers" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zombie Carriage Drivers.png" data-image-key="Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231129024717" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png/revision/latest?cb=20231129024717" class="image"><img alt="Zombie Carriage Drivers" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231129024717" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zombie Carriage Drivers.png" data-image-key="Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231129024717" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zombie_Carriage_Drivers.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hunchback, his steed, and Centaur</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The carriage drivers were a group of creatures that were first seen pulling the carriage that carried Nami, Usopp and Chopper.<sup id="cite_ref-C,_H,_and_D_intro_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-C,_H,_and_D_intro-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> They consist of a skull-faced, centaur-like creature, a hunchback of sorts, and a sort of stitched up dog. The three Straw Hats they escorted could not get a good look at them and thus they thought the three creatures were some sort of horses. Though the Straw Hats could not get a good look at them, they however sensed something odd about the creatures.
</p><p>The creatures pulled the carriage through the forest and into the cemetery. After they pulled the carriage to the cemetery, they ran away to somewhere else on Thriller Bark.<sup id="cite_ref-C,_H,_and_D_exit_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-C,_H,_and_D_exit-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Oars was defeated, the centaur was among the forest and graveyard zombies expressing their concern. However, as soon as Moria stood back up, he and the other zombies cheered.<sup id="cite_ref-oars_defeated_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oars_defeated-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The shadows animating them were later sucked out of them by their master, Gecko Moria. Without any shadows animating them, they returned to being corpses.<sup id="cite_ref-Shadow_Asgard_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shadow_Asgard-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>They debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_444" title="Chapter 444">Chapter 444</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_340" title="Episode 340">Episode 340</a>. The cloaked hunchback and centaur are voiced by Hirofumi Tanaka and Yoshihiro Kanemitsu in Japanese.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Surprise_Zombies_2">Surprise Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Buhichuck">Buhichuck</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130604225657" class="image"><img alt="Buhichuck Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="162" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Buhichuck Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604225657" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20130604225657" class="image"><img alt="Buhichuck Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604225657" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="162" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Buhichuck Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130604225657" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Buhichuck_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Buhichuck</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Buhichuck" title="Buhichuck">Buhichuck</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Buhichuck is the leader of the surprise zombies in the dining room of Dr. Hogback's mansion. He is a pig's head and body mounted on the wall like a hunting trophy. He has the number 298 printed on his forehead. He is not to be mistaken for a wild zombie even though he is actually an animal.
</p><p>He first appeared in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_446" title="Chapter 446">Chapter 446</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_340" title="Episode 340">Episode 340</a>. He is voiced by Keiji Hirai in Japanese and Matt Thurston in the FUNimation English dub.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rug_Bear">Rug Bear</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Bear_Skin_Rug.png/revision/latest?cb=20180719034829" class="image"><img alt="Bear Skin Rug" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="208" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bear Skin Rug.png" data-image-key="Bear_Skin_Rug.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Bear_Skin_Rug.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180719034829" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Bear_Skin_Rug.png/revision/latest?cb=20180719034829" class="image"><img alt="Bear Skin Rug" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Bear_Skin_Rug.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180719034829" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="208" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bear Skin Rug.png" data-image-key="Bear_Skin_Rug.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Bear_Skin_Rug.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180719034829" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bear_Skin_Rug.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rug Bear Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><b>Rug Bear</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">敷きグマ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Shikiguma</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span><sup id="cite_ref-BlueDeep_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BlueDeep-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> was first seen in the dining hall of Hogback's mansion.<sup id="cite_ref-Bear_Rug_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bear_Rug-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> It was later revealed to be some sort of flat zombie creature during the skirmish with the painting zombies and Nami, Usopp and Chopper.<sup id="cite_ref-Bear_Rug_alive_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bear_Rug_alive-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Later, when the rest of the Straw Hats entered the mansion and fought with the painting zombies in the dining hall, it was defeated by Luffy with Gomu Gomu no Bazooka.<sup id="cite_ref-Paint_Zombies_vs._5_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paint_Zombies_vs._5-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Luffy, upon defeating it also commented that if they weren't enemies he would've asked it to join his crew.
</p><p>He later reappeared among the surprise zombies screaming in surprise at Oars being knocked down by Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-oars_falls_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oars_falls-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He first appeared in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_446" title="Chapter 446">Chapter 446</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_341" title="Episode 341">Episode 341</a>. He is voiced by Eiji Takemoto in Japanese.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jack-in-the-Box">Jack-in-the-Box</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter of the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_432" title="Chapter 432">chapter 432</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914015652" class="image"><img alt="Jack in the Box Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="94" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jack in the Box Zombie.png" data-image-key="Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914015652" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914015652" class="image"><img alt="Jack in the Box Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914015652" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="94" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jack in the Box Zombie.png" data-image-key="Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914015652" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jack_in_the_Box_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jack-in-the-Box Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <b>Jack-in-the-Box</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">びっくり箱</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Bikkuri Bako</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Surprise Box")</span> is a demented-looking, stitched-up clown creature that resides in a box located in Hogback's room.<sup id="cite_ref-Jack_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jack-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> In the manga, it has several nails embedded in its head while in the anime, it has none. It was discovered by Nami, Usopp, and Chopper when they opened the box in hopes of finding treasure. It has the number 256 printed on its collar. While the box it was in had nothing else in it, it however commented that a treasure of some sort is hidden somewhere else on the island. This comment interested Nami very much.
</p><p>He debuted in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_448" title="Chapter 448">Chapter 448</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_342" title="Episode 342">Episode 342</a>. He is voiced by Eiji Takemoto in Japanese.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wall_Zombie">Wall Zombie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Wall_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130902005944" class="image"><img alt="Wall Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wall Zombie.png" data-image-key="Wall_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Wall_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130902005944" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Wall_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130902005944" class="image"><img alt="Wall Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Wall_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130902005944" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wall Zombie.png" data-image-key="Wall_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Wall_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130902005944" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wall_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Wall Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <b>Wall Zombie</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">壁ゾンビ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kabe Zonbi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> is a zombie that is basically a block of stone with arms stitched on. Its most distinguishing feature is a human face stretched out and stitched to its surface. It first appeared by the order of Buhichuck to block a doorway in order to prevent Luffy and the two Straw Hats with him from escaping from the Zombie Generals.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Wall_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Wall-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> It may be based on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nurikabe_(folklore)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nurikabe (folklore)">nurikabe</a> from Japanese folklore.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soldier_Zombies_2">Soldier Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Victoria_Cindry">Victoria Cindry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119053610" class="image"><img alt="Victoria Cindry Zombie Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Victoria Cindry Zombie Portrait.png" data-image-key="Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119053610" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119053610" class="image"><img alt="Victoria Cindry Zombie Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119053610" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Victoria Cindry Zombie Portrait.png" data-image-key="Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119053610" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Victoria_Cindry_Zombie_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Victoria Cindry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Cindry" title="Victoria Cindry">Victoria Cindry</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Victoria Cindry is a servant to Dr. Hogback, she was a former actress whose tragic death forced the doctor to work with Moria to turn her into his personal zombie assistant. The shadow placed inside her made her have an immense hatred for plates.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span id="Gyoro.2C_Nin.2C_and_Bao"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Gyoro,_Nin,_and_Bao">Gyoro, Nin, and Bao</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20140916083249" class="image"><img alt="Gyoro, Nin, and Bao Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gyoro, Nin, and Bao Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140916083249" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20140916083249" class="image"><img alt="Gyoro, Nin, and Bao Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140916083249" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gyoro, Nin, and Bao Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Gyoro%2C_Nin%2C_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140916083249" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gyoro,_Nin,_and_Bao_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Gyoro, Nin, and Bao</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Gyoro,_Nin,_and_Bao" title="Gyoro, Nin, and Bao">Gyoro, Nin, and Bao</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Gyoro, Nin, and Bao are trio of oddly shaped zombie creatures that were first seen reporting to Gecko Moria about the Straw Hats' arrival.<sup id="cite_ref-Three_fruits_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Three_fruits-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tailor_Zombie">Tailor Zombie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Tailor_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20180717100304" class="image"><img alt="Tailor Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="231" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tailor Zombie.png" data-image-key="Tailor_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Tailor_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180717100304" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Tailor_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20180717100304" class="image"><img alt="Tailor Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Tailor_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180717100304" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="231" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tailor Zombie.png" data-image-key="Tailor_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Tailor_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180717100304" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tailor_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tailor Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The tailor zombie is a zombie that serves as the tailor on Thriller Bark. He is a short old man with gray hair and wears a red bowtie. He was also able to remove his eye from its socket. He was first seen when Absalom carried in an unconscious Nami in to take her measurements for the wedding dress. Upon being asked about the wedding preparations, he responded by stating that they were ready as always.<sup id="cite_ref-wedding_preparations_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wedding_preparations-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, a scene is added in which he whips the two painting zombies with his tape measure to prevent them from peeping on Nami as he changed her into her wedding dress. He does this as he knows that Absalom was secretly still in the room waiting to see Nami be changed and so warns the paintings that they would be in trouble if they actually saw Nami being changed.<sup id="cite_ref-wedding_dress_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wedding_dress-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He first appeared in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_458" title="Chapter 458">Chapter 458</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_352" title="Episode 352">Episode 352</a>. He is voiced by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keiichi_Sonobe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Keiichi Sonobe">Keiichi Sonobe</a> in the Japanese anime.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pastor_Zombie">Pastor Zombie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Pastor_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20180717100427" class="image"><img alt="Pastor Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="286" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pastor Zombie.png" data-image-key="Pastor_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Pastor_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180717100427" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Pastor_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20180717100427" class="image"><img alt="Pastor Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Pastor_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180717100427" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="286" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pastor Zombie.png" data-image-key="Pastor_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Pastor_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180717100427" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pastor_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pastor Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The pastor zombie is a zombie that serves as the pastor on Thriller Bark. He is a skinny old man that wears a tall hat with a cross on it. He is also dressed in the typical garments for a priest. He was first seen when Absalom carried in an unconscious Nami in to take her measurements for the wedding dress.<sup id="cite_ref-wedding_preparations_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wedding_preparations-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Later, he is seen at the ceremonial hall in charge of the wedding ceremony, as Absalom and an unconscious Nami exchange their vows.<sup id="cite_ref-wedding_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wedding-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> However, before the two can kiss, Sanji shows up and stops the wedding. Throughout Sanji and Absalom's fights, the pastor and a fellow zombie are constantly in surprise at both Sanji and Absalom's pervertedness and the fact that Sanji was able to attack Absalom at ease.
</p><p>Later, in the confusion after Oars destroys the hall, Absalom and the pastor escape to a random room to continue the ceremony. However, Nami suddenly awakes and shocks Absalom unconscious to which the pastor replies by taking note that Absalom had long been weakened after his fight with Sanji.<sup id="cite_ref-wedding_over_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wedding_over-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He first appeared in Chapter 458 and <a href="/wiki/Episode_353" title="Episode 353">Episode 353</a>. He is voiced by Eiji Takemoto in the Japanese anime.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="General_Zombies_2">General Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ryuma">Ryuma</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119071210" class="image"><img alt="Ryuma (Zombie) Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ryuma (Zombie) Portrait.png" data-image-key="Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071210" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119071210" class="image"><img alt="Ryuma (Zombie) Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071210" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ryuma (Zombie) Portrait.png" data-image-key="Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Ryuma_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071210" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ryuma_(Zombie)_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ryuma</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Ryuma_(Zombie)" title="Ryuma (Zombie)">Ryuma (Zombie)</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Ryuma was a legendary <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> from <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano</a>'s distant past. When Gecko Moria attacked the Wano Country, he managed to steal Ryuma's corpse as well as his sword, <a href="/wiki/Shusui" title="Shusui">Shusui</a>. He kept the body for a while until he encountered <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a>, whose shadow he took to place in Ryuma. Brook attempted to take back his shadow a few times, but Ryuma always overpowered him. However, after a battle with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, Ryuma's corpse was burnt to ashes, thus returning Brook's shadow to him.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="John">John</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/John_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20190602033155" class="image"><img alt="John Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="John Portrait.png" data-image-key="John_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/John_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190602033155" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/John_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20190602033155" class="image"><img alt="John Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/John_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190602033155" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="John Portrait.png" data-image-key="John_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/John_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190602033155" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:John_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Captain John</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/John" title="John">John</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>John was once a member of the infamous <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> until its disbandment. He became a pirate captain and amassed a lot of treasure, but was killed by his own crew for his loathsome ways. His body was found by Moria and animated with the shadow of a drunkard.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Lola">Lola</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/19/Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119072154" class="image"><img alt="Lola (Zombie) Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lola (Zombie) Portrait.png" data-image-key="Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/19/Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119072154" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/19/Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119072154" class="image"><img alt="Lola (Zombie) Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/19/Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119072154" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lola (Zombie) Portrait.png" data-image-key="Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/19/Lola_%28Zombie%29_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119072154" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lola_(Zombie)_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lola</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Lola_(Zombie)" title="Lola (Zombie)">Lola (Zombie)</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Lola is large warthog zombie that is animated by a <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Lola" title="Charlotte Lola">pirate woman of the same name</a>. She frequently attempts to marry <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a>, but is rejected every time. She then ends up becoming friends with <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>, and that friendship transferred to the real Lola when her shadow was returned.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jigoro">Jigoro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Jigoro_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119071456" class="image"><img alt="Jigoro Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jigoro Portrait.png" data-image-key="Jigoro_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Jigoro_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071456" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Jigoro_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119071456" class="image"><img alt="Jigoro Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Jigoro_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071456" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jigoro Portrait.png" data-image-key="Jigoro_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Jigoro_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200119071456" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jigoro_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jigoro</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Jigoro" title="Jigoro">Jigoro</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Jigoro was a powerful swordsman in life. After his death, Moria found his corpse and eventually used Zoro's shadow to animate it, making him a powerful swordsman who can use <a href="/wiki/Three_Sword_Style" title="Three Sword Style">Three Sword Style</a>.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tararan">Tararan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0b/Tararan_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731030928" class="image"><img alt="Tararan Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tararan Portrait.png" data-image-key="Tararan_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0b/Tararan_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180731030928" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0b/Tararan_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731030928" class="image"><img alt="Tararan Portrait" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0b/Tararan_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180731030928" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tararan Portrait.png" data-image-key="Tararan_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0b/Tararan_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180731030928" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tararan_Portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tararan</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Tararan" title="Tararan">Tararan</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>A large spider-monkey hybrid, Tararan was in charge of the Spider-Mice, who were in charge of capturing victims and bring them to Moria in order to steal their shadows. However, he was defeated and purified by Brook.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>

</p><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_Ranked_Zombies_2">Special Ranked Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Oars">Oars</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Oars_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230528185603" class="image"><img alt="Oars Anime Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="193" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Oars Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Oars_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Oars_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230528185603" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Oars_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230528185603" class="image"><img alt="Oars Anime Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Oars_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230528185603" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="193" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Oars Anime Infobox.png" data-image-key="Oars_Anime_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Oars_Anime_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230528185603" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Oars_Anime_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Oars</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>A legendary Ancient Giant from the distant past, Oars was famed for his strength until he froze to death while trying to prove his might. His body was preserved in ice until it was eventually obtained by Moria and modified by Hogback. After taking <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>'s shadow, he used it to animate Oars' body. Oars managed to defeat a majority of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> until he was defeated by the real Luffy (who was powered up by 100 shadows at the time), and then defeated once more by the entire crew.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjecturally-Named_Zombies">Conjecturally-Named Zombies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Zebra_Kangaroo_.28.2336.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Zebra_Kangaroo_(#36)">Zebra Kangaroo (#36)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Zebra_Roo.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20180716033755" class="image"><img alt="Zebra Roo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="187" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zebra Roo.PNG" data-image-key="Zebra_Roo.PNG" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Zebra_Roo.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180716033755" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Zebra_Roo.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20180716033755" class="image"><img alt="Zebra Roo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Zebra_Roo.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180716033755" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="187" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zebra Roo.PNG" data-image-key="Zebra_Roo.PNG" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Zebra_Roo.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180716033755" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zebra_Roo.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Boxing Zebra Kangaroo Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The zebra kangaroo is a wild zombie that resembles a kangaroo with zebra skin stripes on its body instead of its regular kangaroo fur. It has a pouch with a zipper on its underside and the number 36 printed on it. It wears a bow tie and is equipped with a pair of orange boxing gloves. It somewhat resembles the typical <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boxing_Kangaroo" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Boxing Kangaroo">boxing kangaroo</a> image commonly used to personify Australia that is seen in various multimedia.
</p><p>It first appeared in the group of Wild Zombies that appeared in Perona's Wonder Garden and has been frequently seen among them since.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Wonderland_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Wonderland-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, the kangaroo is given more screen time as he engages Usopp in a boxing match. However, rather than punch Usopp, he accidentally punches Zombies #52 and #154. As a result, he gives chase to both Usopp and Nami across some stairs along with several small Wild Zombies. Although, they were able to escape by jumping onto a separate column, Usopp decided to taunt the Zebra Kangaroo. This causes it to be angered and it decides to jump across the columns to reach the two. Ultimately, it is shot down by Usopp mid-air as it was jumping towards them.<sup id="cite_ref-Kangaroo_zebra_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kangaroo_zebra-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>Later, it appears to have recovered from its fall and appears in Perona's room when Zoro, Sanji, Franky and Usopp stumble in.
</p><p>Afterwards, it reappears alongside the other wild zombies attempting to wake up an unconscious Perona.
</p>
<h4><span id="Lion-Cow_.28.2337.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Lion-Cow_(#37)">Lion-Cow (#37)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Lion-cow_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024729" class="image"><img alt="Lion-cow Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="185" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lion-cow Zombie.png" data-image-key="Lion-cow_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Lion-cow_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914024729" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Lion-cow_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024729" class="image"><img alt="Lion-cow Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Lion-cow_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914024729" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="185" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lion-cow Zombie.png" data-image-key="Lion-cow_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Lion-cow_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914024729" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lion-cow_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lion-Cow Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A zombie that appears to be a small lion of sorts with what looks like the lower half of a cow. It has the number 37 printed on its belly. It was first seen frolicking with a number of other creatures in the forest singing about their "prey" as Nami, Usopp, and Chopper pass by in Hildon's carriage. Upon noticing that they have been seen, they quickly went into hiding.<sup id="cite_ref-TB_woods_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TB_woods-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, it later appears alongside the other forest zombies cheering on the graveyard zombies as they sing their "Zombie Night" song.<sup id="cite_ref-zombie_night_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-zombie_night-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, it was seen amongst the zombies escaping the vicinity of the mansion as Oars began his rampage.<sup id="cite_ref-escape_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-escape-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span id="Manticore_.28.2369.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Manticore_(#69)">Manticore (#69)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Zombie_69.png/revision/latest?cb=20240903212027" class="image"><img alt="Zombie 69" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zombie 69.png" data-image-key="Zombie_69.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Zombie_69.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240903212027" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Zombie_69.png/revision/latest?cb=20240903212027" class="image"><img alt="Zombie 69" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Zombie_69.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240903212027" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zombie 69.png" data-image-key="Zombie_69.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Zombie_69.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240903212027" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zombie_69.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Manticore Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>This zombie is a lion with a man's face stitched to its body that Nami saw.<sup id="cite_ref-Manticore_intro_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Manticore_intro-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> It resembles a manticore, a type of lion with the face of a man, the tail of a scorpion, and the occasional wings of a dragon. It has the number 69 printed on its hind quarters. Upon seeing this beast, Nami tried to convince Usopp and Chopper of what she saw with an apparently bad drawing (which somewhat looked like <a href="/wiki/Mohji" title="Mohji">Mohji</a>). Its mouth was removed and placed on Absalom's face. This beast is different from the <a href="/wiki/Manticores" class="mw-redirect" title="Manticores">Manticores</a> of <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>, though they do look somewhat similar.
</p><p>Comparisons between this manticore's lion faced stitches and Absalom's were often noted. Oda later confirmed that the Manticore's face was indeed used on Absalom's face by Hogback. However, the Manticore's human face was never Absalom's. Absalom's human face may be on another zombie elsewhere. While answering this question, Oda also noted that Absalom has very few Japanese fans and was reluctant to say more on the matter.<sup id="cite_ref-Volume_48_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Volume_48-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Giant_Earthworm_.28.23159.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Giant_Earthworm_(#159)">Giant Earthworm (#159)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Earthworm_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024626" class="image"><img alt="Earthworm Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="170" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Earthworm Zombie.png" data-image-key="Earthworm_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Earthworm_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914024626" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Earthworm_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914024626" class="image"><img alt="Earthworm Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Earthworm_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914024626" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="170" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Earthworm Zombie.png" data-image-key="Earthworm_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Earthworm_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914024626" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Earthworm_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Giant Earthworm Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>This is a zombie that appears to be a giant earthworm. It has what appears to be a human head stitched on to one end as its face. It has the number 159 on its body. It was first seen frolicking with a number of other creatures in the forest singing about their "prey" as Nami, Usopp, and Chopper pass by in Hildon's carriage. Upon noticing that they have been seen, they quickly went into hiding.<sup id="cite_ref-TB_woods_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TB_woods-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, it later appears alongside the other forest zombies cheering on the graveyard zombies as they sing their "Zombie Night" song.<sup id="cite_ref-zombie_night_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-zombie_night-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span id="Cheshire_Cat_.28.23193.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Cheshire_Cat_(#193)">Cheshire Cat (#193)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914025517" class="image"><img alt="Chesire Cat Zombie" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Chesire Cat Zombie.png" data-image-key="Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914025517" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png/revision/latest?cb=20130914025517" class="image"><img alt="Chesire Cat Zombie" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914025517" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Chesire Cat Zombie.png" data-image-key="Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130914025517" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Chesire_Cat_Zombie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Cheshire Cat Zombie</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>This zombie is a stitched up cat wearing what appears to be a pilot's cap. It has the number 193 on its hind quarters. It was first seen frolicking with a number of other creatures in the forest singing about their "prey" as Nami, Usopp, and Chopper pass by in Hildon's carriage. Upon noticing that they have been seen, they quickly went into hiding.<sup id="cite_ref-TB_woods_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TB_woods-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> It was later seen roaming a hallway in <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Mansion" class="mw-redirect" title="Thriller Bark Mansion">Hogback's mansion</a> as Usopp and Chopper were guarding Nami while she was taking a bath.<sup id="cite_ref-Cheshire_Cat_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cheshire_Cat-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, it later appears alongside the other forest zombies cheering on the graveyard zombies as they sing their "Zombie Night" song.<sup id="cite_ref-zombie_night_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-zombie_night-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p><p>When Oars was defeated, the cat zombie was among the forest and graveyard zombies expressing their concern. However, as soon as Moria stood back up, he and the other zombies cheered.<sup id="cite_ref-oars_defeated_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oars_defeated-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Its disturbingly wide grin apparently makes it look like the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cheshire_Cat" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cheshire Cat">Cheshire Cat</a> from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alice%27s_Adventures_in_Wonderland" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alice&#39;s Adventures in Wonderland">Alice's Adventures in Wonderland</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FZombie%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>When the zombies are ordered to commence the attack on the Straw Hats, they perform a little disco ball aided dance reminiscent of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Jackson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Michael Jackson">Michael Jackson</a>'s <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thriller_(song)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thriller (song)">Thriller</a></i>. While the manga's depiction of the dance was just a single panel and the song the zombies sang was just a few lines, the dance was expanded in anime. In the anime, it is a full-blown dance number called "<a href="/wiki/Zombie_Night" title="Zombie Night">Zombie Night</a>" wherein the zombies danced and sang to a tune reminiscent of 70s disco music.<sup id="cite_ref-Zombie_Night_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zombie_Night-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Some zombies not only shared another zombie's number, but they often changed their numbers over the course of their appearance. Furthermore, some zombies did not even have their manga counterpart's number.</li>
<li>The zombies frequently add the adjective "rotting"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">腐る</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kusage</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> as an intensifier to their speech (<i>e.g.</i> "that's rotting bad").</li>
<li>Several characters have indicated that zombie fiction is common throughout the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a>, even citing genre clichés such as zombies being able to "infect" living creatures through bites. It remains unknown whether the Kage Kage no Mi and its "real" zombies had any effect in shaping these.</li>
<li>Before <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">canonical</a> zombies (and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a>) were introduced in the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Arc" title="Thriller Bark Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</a>, the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Anime)" title="One Piece (Anime)">anime</a> explored the idea of animate corpses in at least two original productions: <a href="/wiki/Joke" title="Joke">Joke</a> in <a href="/wiki/Episode_Special_1" title="Episode Special 1">the first TV special</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Red_Arrow_Pirates" class="mw-redirect" title="Red Arrow Pirates">Red Arrow Pirates</a> in <a href="/wiki/Baron_Omatsuri_and_the_Secret_Island" title="Baron Omatsuri and the Secret Island">the sixth movie</a>. Neither production, however, uses the term <i>zombie</i>.</li></ul>
